================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/RCMP_ERT/RCMP_ERT_F-150/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → RCMP:ERT → RCMP:ERT F-150 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:45
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/RCMP_ERT/RCMP_ERT_F-150/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → RCMP:ERT → RCMP:ERT F-150 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:45
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/RCMP_ERT/RCMP_ERT_F-150/Config/Modules/Spotlight.lua ---

--[[
    Spotlight (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → RCMP:ERT → RCMP:ERT F-150 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:45
]]
			return function (spotlight, event, subevent, angle)
				
				local Spotlight = spotlight;
				local Beam = spotlight.Center.Casing.LightBeam;
				local Light = spotlight.Center.Casing.Light;
				
				local Hinge = Spotlight.Center.Pivot.HingeConstraint;
				
				if subevent == 'Enable' then
				
					Light.Enabled = event;
					Beam.Enabled = event;
					spotlight.Center.LED1.Material = (event == true and Enum.Material.Neon) or Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
					
				elseif subevent == 'Rotate' then
					if angle == 'Left' then
						Hinge.TargetAngle = 90;
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
					elseif angle == 'Right' then
						Hinge.TargetAngle = -80;
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
					elseif angle == 'Halt' then
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 0;
					end;
				end;
			end;

--[[
    Pattern1 (ModuleScript)

    Parent: ELSPatterns
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:45

local elsModule = require(script.Parent.Parent.Modules.ElsPart);

return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	--Front Lightbar lights
	local T1 = elsModule(ELSModel.T1)
	local T2 = elsModule(ELSModel.T2)
	local T3 = elsModule(ELSModel.T3)
	local T4 = elsModule(ELSModel.T4)
	local T5 = elsModule(ELSModel.T5)
	local T6 = elsModule(ELSModel.T6)
	local T7 = elsModule(ELSModel.T7)
	local T8 = elsModule(ELSModel.T8)

	--Front lights
	local F1 = elsModule(ELSModel.F1)
	local F2 = elsModule(ELSModel.F2)
	local F3 = elsModule(ELSModel.F3)
	local F4 = elsModule(ELSModel.F4)

	--Back lights lights
	local R1 = elsModule(ELSModel.R1)
	local R2 = elsModule(ELSModel.R2) 
	local R3 = elsModule(ELSModel.R3)
	local R4 = elsModule(ELSModel.R4)
	local R5 = elsModule(ELSModel.R5)
	local R6 = elsModule(ELSModel.R6)
	local R7 = elsModule(ELSModel.R7)
	local R8 = elsModule(ELSModel.R8)

	if enabled then
		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()			
				while true do
				F1(1);	
				F2(1);	
				F3(1);	
				F4(1);					
				wait()						
				end
			end)
		end)()
		
		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()			
				while true do
				T1(1);
				T2(1);
				T3(1);
				T4(1);
				T5(1);
				T6(1);
				T7(1);
				T8(1);		
				wait()	
				end
			end)
		end)()		

		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()			
				while true do
					R1(0 ,Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					R2(0 ,Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					R3(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					R4(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));	
					R5(1 ,Color3.fromRGB(82, 124, 174));
					R6(1 ,Color3.fromRGB(82, 124, 174));
					R7(1, Color3.fromRGB(82, 124, 174));
					R8(1, Color3.fromRGB(82, 124, 174));						
					wait(0.15)						

					R1(1);
					R2(1);
					R3(1);
					R4(1);
					R5(1);
					R6(1);
					R7(1);
					R8(1);			
					wait(0.02)		

					R1(0);
					R2(0);
					R3(0);
					R4(0);
					R5(1);
					R6(1);
					R7(1);
					R8(1);			
					wait(0.15)		

					R1(1);
					R2(1);
					R3(1);
					R4(1);
					R5(1);
					R6(1);
					R7(1);
					R8(1);			
					wait(0.02)			

					R1(1);
					R2(1);
					R3(1);
					R4(1);
					R5(0);
					R6(0);
					R7(0);
					R8(0);			
					wait(0.15)		

					R1(1);
					R2(1);
					R3(1);
					R4(1);
					R5(1);
					R6(1);
					R7(1);
					R8(1);			
					wait(0.02)			

					R1(1);
					R2(1);
					R3(1);
					R4(1);
					R5(0);
					R6(0);
					R7(0);
					R8(0);			
					wait(0.15)		

					R1(1);
					R2(1);
					R3(1);
					R4(1);
					R5(1);
					R6(1);
					R7(1);
					R8(1);			
					wait(0.02)		
				end
			end)
		end)()		
				
		
	else
		T1(1 ,Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
		T2(1 ,Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
		T3(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
		T4(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));	
		T5(1, Color3.fromRGB(74, 116, 255));

	end
end

local elsModule = require(script.Parent.Parent.Modules.ElsPart);

return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	--Front Lightbar lights
	local T1 = elsModule(ELSModel.T1)
	local T2 = elsModule(ELSModel.T2)
	local T3 = elsModule(ELSModel.T3)
	local T4 = elsModule(ELSModel.T4)
	local T5 = elsModule(ELSModel.T5)
	local T6 = elsModule(ELSModel.T6)
	local T7 = elsModule(ELSModel.T7)
	local T8 = elsModule(ELSModel.T8)

	--Front lights
	local F1 = elsModule(ELSModel.F1)
	local F2 = elsModule(ELSModel.F2)
	local F3 = elsModule(ELSModel.F3)
	local F4 = elsModule(ELSModel.F4)

	--Back lights lights
	local R1 = elsModule(ELSModel.R1)
	local R2 = elsModule(ELSModel.R2) 
	local R3 = elsModule(ELSModel.R3)
	local R4 = elsModule(ELSModel.R4)
	local R5 = elsModule(ELSModel.R5)
	local R6 = elsModule(ELSModel.R6)
	local R7 = elsModule(ELSModel.R7)
	local R8 = elsModule(ELSModel.R8)

	if enabled then
		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()			
				while true do
				F1(0, Color3.fromRGB(82, 124, 174));
				F2(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				F3(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				F4(0, Color3.fromRGB(82, 124, 174));					
				wait(0.15)						
					
				F1(1);	
				F2(1);	
				F3(1);	
				F4(1);					
				wait(0.12)						
						
				F1(0);	
				F2(1);	
				F3(1);	
				F4(0);					
				wait(0.15)					
					
				F1(1);	
				F2(1);	
				F3(1);	
				F4(1);

			end)
		end)()		
				
		
	else

		T2(1 ,Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
		T3(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));

		T6(1, Color3.fromRGB(74, 116, 255));
		T7(1, Color3.fromRGB(74, 116, 255));
		T8(1, Color3.fromRGB(74, 116, 255));						
		R1(1)
		R2(1)
		R3(1)
		R4(1)
		R5(1)
		R6(1)
		R7(1)
		R8(1)		
		F1(1)
		F2(1)
		F3(1)
		F4(1)
	end
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/RCMP_ERT/RCMP_ERT_F-350/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → RCMP:ERT → RCMP:ERT F-350 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:45
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/RCMP_ERT/RCMP_ERT_F-350/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → RCMP:ERT → RCMP:ERT F-350 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:45
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/RCMP_ERT/RCMP_ERT_F-350/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → RCMP:ERT → RCMP:ERT F-350 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:45
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/RCMP_ERT/RCMP_ERT_F-350/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → RCMP:ERT → RCMP:ERT F-350 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:45
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/RCMP_ERT/RCMP_ERT_F-350/Config/Modules/Reverselights.lua ---

--[[
    Reverselights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → RCMP:ERT → RCMP:ERT F-350 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:45
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local reverselights = body.Reverselights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/RCMP_ERT/RCMP_ERT_F-350/Config/Modules/Spotlight.lua ---

--[[
    Spotlight (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → RCMP:ERT → RCMP:ERT F-350 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:45
]]
return function (spotlight, event, subevent, angle)
	
	local Spotlight = spotlight;
	local Beam = spotlight.Center.Casing.LightBeam;
	local Light = spotlight.Center.Casing.Light;
	
	local Hinge = Spotlight.Center.Pivot.HingeConstraint;
	
	if subevent == 'Enable' then
	
		Light.Enabled = event;
		Beam.Enabled = event;
		spotlight.Center.LED1.Material = (event == true and Enum.Material.Neon) or Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
		
	elseif subevent == 'Rotate' then
		if angle == 'Left' then
			Hinge.TargetAngle = 90;
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
		elseif angle == 'Right' then
			Hinge.TargetAngle = -80;
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
		elseif angle == 'Halt' then
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 0;
		end;
	end;
end;

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/RCMP_ERT/RCMP_ERT_F-350_Closed_back/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → RCMP:ERT → RCMP:ERT F-350 Closed back → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:45
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/RCMP_ERT/RCMP_ERT_F-350_Closed_back/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → RCMP:ERT → RCMP:ERT F-350 Closed back → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:45
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		part.Transparency = (transparency)
		if colour then
			if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
				part.BrickColor = colour;
			elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
				part.Color = colour;
			end;
		end;
		if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
			local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
			a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
			if colour then
				a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
			end
		end;
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/RCMP_ERT/RCMP_ERT_F-350_Closed_back/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → RCMP:ERT → RCMP:ERT F-350 Closed back → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:45
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/RCMP_ERT/RCMP_ERT_F-350_Closed_back/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → RCMP:ERT → RCMP:ERT F-350 Closed back → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:45
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;
